# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/terraform--v1.10.3`
- Use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/terraform--v1.10.3$` filter in keyword_search
- Use `github.com/sg-evals/terraform--v1.10.3` as the `repo` parameter for go_to_definition/find_references/read_file


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

**Sourcegraph Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/terraform--v1.10.3`

# Task: Implement CompactDiffFormatter for Terraform

## Objective
Create a `CompactDiffFormatter` in `internal/command/format/` that produces a condensed,
summary-style diff output for `terraform plan`, showing only resource-level changes
without attribute-level detail.

## Requirements

1. **Create `internal/command/format/compact.go`** with:
   - `CompactDiffFormatter` struct implementing a plan formatter
   - `Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *terraform.Schemas)` method returning string
   - Outputs one line per resource change: `[action] resource_type.name`
   - Groups changes by action type (create/update/delete/replace)
   - Shows summary counts at the end

2. **Create `internal/command/format/compact_test.go`** with tests

3. **Follow Terraform patterns**:
   - Study the existing `DiffFormatter` in the format package
   - Use `plans.Action` constants (Create, Update, Delete, etc.)
   - Use `addrs.AbsResourceInstance` for resource addressing

## Key Reference Files
- `internal/command/format/diff.go` — existing diff formatter
- `internal/command/format/state.go` — state formatter pattern
- `internal/plans/changes.go` — plan change types
- `internal/plans/plan.go` — Plan struct definition
- `internal/addrs/resource.go` — resource addressing

## Success Criteria
- CompactDiffFormatter struct exists in format package
- Format method accepts plan and schemas parameters
- Outputs resource-level change summary
- Groups by action type
- Test file exists

     1→// Copyright (c) HashiCorp, Inc.
     2→// SPDX-License-Identifier: BUSL-1.1
     3→
     4→// Package format contains helpers for formatting various Terraform
     5→// structures for human-readabout output.
     6→//
     7→// This package is used by the official Terraform CLI in formatting any
     8→// output and is exported to encourage non-official frontends to mimic the
     9→// output formatting as much as possible so that text formats of Terraform
    10→// structures have a consistent look and feel.
    11→package format
    12→
    13→import "github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/plans"
    14→
    15→// DiffActionSymbol returns a string that, once passed through a
    16→// colorstring.Colorize, will produce a result that can be written
    17→// to a terminal to produce a symbol made of three printable
    18→// characters, possibly interspersed with VT100 color codes.
    19→func DiffActionSymbol(action plans.Action) string {
    20→	switch action {
    21→	case plans.DeleteThenCreate:
    22→		return "[red]-[reset]/[green]+[reset]"
    23→	case plans.CreateThenDelete:
    24→		return "[green]+[reset]/[red]-[reset]"
    25→	case plans.Create:
    26→		return "  [green]+[reset]"
    27→	case plans.Delete:
    28→		return "  [red]-[reset]"
    29→	case plans.Forget:
    30→		return " [red].[reset]"
    31→	case plans.CreateThenForget:
    32→		return " [green]+[reset]/[red].[reset]"
    33→	case plans.Read:
    34→		return " [cyan]<=[reset]"
    35→	case plans.Update:
    36→		return "  [yellow]~[reset]"
    37→	case plans.NoOp:
    38→		return "   "
    39→	default:
    40→		return "  ?"
    41→	}
    42→}
    43→

// Copyright (c) HashiCorp, Inc.
// SPDX-License-Identifier: BUSL-1.1

package plans

import (
	"fmt"
	"testing"

	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/lang/marks"
	"github.com/zclconf/go-cty/cty"
)

func TestChangeEncodeSensitive(t *testing.T) {
	testVals := []cty.Value{
		cty.ObjectVal(map[string]cty.Value{
			"ding": cty.StringVal("dong").Mark(marks.Sensitive),
		}),
		cty.StringVal("bleep").Mark(marks.Sensitive),
		cty.ListVal([]cty.Value{cty.UnknownVal(cty.String).Mark(marks.Sensitive)}),
	}

	for _, v := range testVals {
		t.Run(fmt.Sprintf("%#v", v), func(t *testing.T) {
			change := Change{
				Before: cty.NullVal(v.Type()),
				After:  v,
			}

			encoded, err := change.Encode(v.Type())
			if err != nil {
				t.Fatal(err)
			}

			decoded, err := encoded.Decode(v.Type())
			if err != nil {
				t.Fatal(err)
			}

			if !v.RawEquals(decoded.After) {
				t.Fatalf("%#v != %#v\n", decoded.After, v)
			}
		})
	}
}

// make sure we get a valid value back even when faced with an error
func TestChangeEncodeError(t *testing.T) {
	changes := &Changes{
		Outputs: []*OutputChange{
			{
				// Missing Addr
				Change: Change{
					Before: cty.NullVal(cty.DynamicPseudoType),
					// can't encode a marked value
					After: cty.StringVal("test").Mark("shoult not be here"),
				},
			},
		},
	}
	// no resources so we can get by with no schemas
	changesSrc, err := changes.Encode(nil)
	if err == nil {
		t.Fatal("expected error")
	}
	if changesSrc == nil {
		t.Fatal("changesSrc should not be nil")
	}
}

### 1. **`internal/command/format/compact.go`**
Contains:
- `CompactDiffFormatter` struct that implements the plan formatter
- `Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string` method that:
  - Groups resource changes by action type (Create, Update, Delete, etc.)
  - Displays changes in a consistent, predefined order
  - Sorts resources alphabetically within each action group
  - Outputs one line per resource change with action symbols
  - Includes a summary section with counts for each action
- `actionName()` helper function that returns human-readable names for each action

### 2. **`internal/command/format/compact_test.go`**
Contains comprehensive tests:
- `TestCompactDiffFormatter_Format` with multiple test cases:
  - Empty plan handling
  - Single create operation
  - Mixed actions (create/update/delete)
  - Multiple resources with the same action (validates sorting)
- `TestCompactDiffFormatter_ActionName` testing all action types
- `mustParseResourceInstanceAddr` helper for test setup

### Key Features:
✅ Condensed, summary-style diff output
✅ Resource-level changes without attribute detail
✅ Groups by action type with human-readable headers
✅ Shows summary counts at the end
✅ Follows Terraform code patterns and style
✅ Handles nil inputs gracefully
✅ Sorts resources for consistent output
✅ Uses existing `DiffActionSymbol()` for consistent formatting

The implementation is ready to use and follows all Terraform conventions and patterns found in the existing codebase.

New Action\n328: //\t--------+-------------+-----------\n329: //\tCreate    true          NoOp\n330: //\tDelete    false         NoOp\n331: //\tReplace   true          Delete\n332: //\tReplace   false         Create\n333: //\n334: // For any combination not in the above table, the Simplify just returns the\n335: // receiver as-is.\n336: func (rc *ResourceInstanceChange) Simplify(destroying bool) 1. WRITE /workspace/internal/command/format/compact.go
// Copyright (c) HashiCorp, Inc.
// SPDX-License-Identifier: BUSL-1.1

package format

import (
	"fmt"
	"sort"
	"strings"

	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/addrs"
	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/plans"
	"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/schemarepo"
)

// CompactDiffFormatter formats a plan as a condensed summary, showing only
// resource-level changes without attribute details.
type CompactDiffFormatter struct{}

// Format takes a plan and schemas and returns a compact diff summary.
// It groups changes by action type and shows a summary count at the end.
func (c *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string {
	if plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {
		return ""
	}

	// Group changes by action
	changes := make(map[plans.Action][]*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc)

	for _, rc := range plan.Changes.Resources {
		changes[rc.Change.Action] = append(changes[rc.Change.Action], rc)
	}

	// Define the order we want to display actions
	actionOrder := []plans.Action{
		plans.Create,
		plans.Update,
		plans.Delete,
		plans.DeleteThenCreate,
		plans.CreateThenDelete,
		plans.Read,
		plans.Forget,
		plans.CreateThenForget,
		plans.NoOp,
	}

	var output strings.Builder
	var totalCounts map[plans.Action]int = make(map[plans.Action]int)

	// Process each action in order
	for _, action := range actionOrder {
		resourceChanges, exists := changes[action]
		if !exists || len(resourceChanges) == 0 {
			continue
		}

		// Sort resources by address for consistent output
		sort.Slice(resourceChanges, func(i, j int) bool {
			return resourceChanges[i].Addr.String() < resourceChanges[j].Addr.String()
		})

		// Write action header
		actionName := actionName(action)
		output.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf("%s:\n", actionName))

		// Write ea
... (truncated)

func TestCompactDiffFormatter_Format(t *testing.T) {
	tests := map[string]struct {
		plan    *plans.Plan
		schemas *schemarepo.Schemas
		want    string
	}{
		"empty plan": {
			plan:    &plans.Plan{Changes: plans.NewChangesSrc()},
			schemas: &schemarepo.Schemas{},
			want:    "",
		},
		"single create": {
			plan: &plans.Plan{
				Changes: &plans.ChangesSrc{
					Resources: []*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc{
						{
							Addr: mustParseResourceInstanceAddr("aws_instance.foo"),
							ChangeSrc: plans.ChangeSrc{
								Action: plans.Create,
								After:  plans.DynamicValue{},
							},
						},
					},
				},
			},
			schemas: &schemarepo.Schemas{},
			want: strings.TrimSpace(`
Create:
  [green]+[reset] aws_instance.foo

Summary:
  Create: 1
`) + "\n",
		},
		"mixed actions": {
			plan: &plans.Plan{
				Changes: &plans.ChangesSrc{
					Resources: []*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc{
						{
							Addr: mustParseResourceInstanceAddr("aws_instance.foo"),
							ChangeSrc: plans.ChangeSrc{
								Action: plans.Create,
								After:  plans.DynamicValue{},

8. EDIT /workspace/internal/command/format/compact_test.go
Before
// Helper function to parse resource instance addresses for testing
func mustParseResourceInstanceAddr(s string) addrs.AbsResourceInstance {
	addr, diags := addrs.ParseAbsResourceInstanceStr(s)
	if diags.HasErrors() {
		panic(diags.Err())
	}
	return addr
}

// Helper to create test DynamicValues
func testDynamicValue(val cty.Value) plans.DynamicValue {
	dv, _ := plans.NewDynamicValue(val, val.Type())
	return dv
}
After
// Helper function to parse resource instance addresses for testing
func mustParseResourceInstanceAddr(s string) addrs.AbsResourceInstance {
	addr, diags := addrs.ParseAbsResourceInstanceStr(s)
	if diags.HasErrors() {
		panic(diags.Err())
	}
	return addr
}
